Greetings to all UTMians,

Attached in the announcement below is the academic Calendar for undergraduate students.

Students can use this calendar to find out important dates for semester 2 session 2021/2022. Students may complete their course registration during the following dates:

With this, we hereby remind students to complete their course registration during these dates to avoid being penalized. We wish you all the best and do your best for semester 2 of the upcoming 2021/2022 session

16/03/2022, 1:13โฏpm - +966 53 161 5517: For deferment applications, students are required to write an official application letter and fill up the deferment form .

1) Official Application letter / Medical report

If the reason for deferment is due to health problems, please provide a medical report, otherwise students need to prepare a letter. 
Address the letter to

        Assoc. Prof. Dr. Mohamed Afendi Bin Mohamed Piah
        Associate  Chair ( Academic & Student Development)
        School of Electrical Engineering, Faculty of Engineering
        Universiti Teknologi Malaysia

Please include the reason you want to defer in the letter. This letter should be verified/recommended by an Academic Advisor.


2. Deferment form ( for International Students)

Attached is the deferment form for international students.

Form guidelines  :
1. Fill and COMPLETE the form. 
2. Read and sign the Student Declaration at Section II
3. Obtain approval from UTM International (ISC) and your Faculty  -  Email to  ayuazrin@utm.my


Submit the COMPLETE form and letter to the Faculty/School Academic Office  - Email back to SKE the approved form from ISC .
Please note that completion of this form does not guarantee that your be granted for deferment

thank you,
